This is a semi-arbitrary value to ensure that a\n\t// certain minimum of nodes are checked for feasibility. This in turn helps\n\t// ensure a minimum level of spreading.\n\tminFeasibleNodesToFind = 100\n\t// minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind is the minimum percentage of nodes that\n\t// would be scored in each scheduling cycle. This is a semi-arbitrary value\n\t// to ensure that a certain minimum of nodes are checked for feasibility.\n\t// This in turn helps ensure a minimum level of spreading.\n\tminFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind = 5\n\t// numberOfHighestScoredNodesToReport is the number of node scores\n\t// to be included in ScheduleResult.\n\tnumberOfHighestScoredNodesToReport = 3\n)\n\n// ScheduleOne does the entire scheduling workflow for a single pod. It is serialized on the scheduling algorithm's host fitting.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) ScheduleOne(ctx context.Context) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tpodInfo, err := sched.NextPod(logger)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error while retrieving next pod from scheduling queue\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\t// pod could be nil when schedulerQueue is closed\n\tif podInfo == nil || podInfo.Pod == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tpod := podInfo.Pod\n\t// TODO(knelasevero): Remove duplicated keys from log entry calls\n\t// When contextualized logging hits GA\n\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/111672\n\tlogger = klog.LoggerWithValues(logger, \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\tctx = klog.NewContext(ctx, logger)\n\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"About to try and schedule pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\n\tfwk, err := sched.frameworkForPod(pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// This shouldn't happen, because we only accept for scheduling the pods\n\t\t// which specify a scheduler name that matches one of the profiles.\n\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error occurred\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif sched.skipPodSchedule(ctx, fwk, pod) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Attempting to schedule pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\n\t// Synchronously attempt to find a fit for the pod.\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\tstate := framework.NewCycleState()\n\tstate.SetRecordPluginMetrics(rand.Intn(100) < pluginMetricsSamplePercent)\n\n\t// Initialize an empty podsToActivate struct, which will be filled up by plugins or stay empty.\n\tpodsToActivate := framework.NewPodsToActivate()\n\tstate.Write(framework.PodsToActivateKey, podsToActivate)\n\n\tschedulingCycleCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\tscheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, status := sched.schedulingCycle(schedulingCycleCtx, state, fwk, podInfo, start, podsToActivate)\n\tif !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\tsched.FailureHandler(schedulingCycleCtx, fwk, assumedPodInfo, status, scheduleResult.nominatingInfo, start)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// bind the pod to its host asynchronously (we can do this b/c of the assumption step above).\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tbindingCycleCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.Binding).Inc()\n\t\tdefer metrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.Binding).Dec()\n\n\t\tstatus := sched.bindingCycle(bindingCycleCtx, state, fwk, scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, start, podsToActivate)\n\t\tif !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t\tsched.handleBindingCycleError(bindingCycleCtx, state, fwk, assumedPodInfo, start, scheduleResult, status)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Usually, DonePod is called inside the scheduling queue,\n\t\t// but in this case, we need to call it here because this Pod won't go back to the scheduling queue.\n\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Done(assumedPodInfo.Pod.UID)\n\t}()\n}\n\nvar clearNominatedNode = &framework.NominatingInfo{NominatingMode: framework.ModeOverride, NominatedNodeName: \"\"}\n\n// schedulingCycle tries to schedule a single Pod.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) schedulingCycle(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n\tstart time.Time,\n\tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate,\n) (ScheduleResult, *framework.QueuedPodInfo, *framework.Status) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tpod := podInfo.Pod\n\tscheduleResult, err := sched.SchedulePod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n\t\t}()\n\t\tif err == ErrNoNodesAvailable {\n\t\t\tstatus := framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable).WithError(err)\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, status\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfitError, ok := err.(*framework.FitError)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error selecting node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, framework.AsStatus(err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// SchedulePod() may have failed because the pod would not fit on any host, so we try to\n\t\t// preempt, with the expectation that the next time the pod is tried for scheduling it\n\t\t// will fit due to the preemption. It is also possible that a different pod will schedule\n\t\t// into the resources that were preempted, but this is harmless.\n\n\t\tif !fwk.HasPostFilterPlugins() {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"No PostFilter plugins are registered, so no preemption will be performed\")\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{}, podInfo, framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Run PostFilter plugins to attempt to make the pod schedulable in a future scheduling cycle.\n\t\tresult, status := fwk.RunPostFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod, fitError.Diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\t\tmsg := status.Message()\n\t\tfitError.Diagnosis.PostFilterMsg = msg\n\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar nominatingInfo *framework.NominatingInfo\n\t\tif result != nil {\n\t\t\tnominatingInfo = result.NominatingInfo\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: nominatingInfo}, podInfo, framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n\t// Tell the cache to assume that a pod now is running on a given node, even though it hasn't been bound yet.\n\t// This allows us to keep scheduling without waiting on binding to occur.\n\tassumedPodInfo := podInfo.DeepCopy()\n\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n\t// assume modifies `assumedPod` by setting NodeName=scheduleResult.SuggestedHost\n\terr = sched.assume(logger, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// This is most probably result of a BUG in retrying logic.\n\t\t// We report an error here so that pod scheduling can be retried.\n\t\t// This relies on the fact that Error will check if the pod has been bound\n\t\t// to a node and if so will not add it back to the unscheduled pods queue\n\t\t// (otherwise this would cause an infinite loop).\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.AsStatus(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Run the Reserve method of reserve plugins.\n\tif sts := fwk.RunReservePluginsReserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !sts.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n\t\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif sts.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n\t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap: framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: sts},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(sts)\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.NewStatus(sts.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, sts\n\t}\n\n\t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n\trunPermitStatus := fwk.RunPermitPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\tif !runPermitStatus.IsWait() && !runPermitStatus.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n\t\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif runPermitStatus.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n\t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap: framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: runPermitStatus},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(runPermitStatus)\n\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.NewStatus(runPermitStatus.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, runPermitStatus\n\t}\n\n\t// At the end of a successful scheduling cycle, pop and move up Pods if needed.\n\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n\t\t// Clear the entries after activation.\n\t\tpodsToActivate.Map = make(map[string]*v1.Pod)\n\t}\n\n\treturn scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, nil\n}\n\n// bindingCycle tries to bind an assumed Pod.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) bindingCycle(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n\tassumedPodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n\tstart time.Time,\n\tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate) *framework.Status {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\n\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n\n\t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n\tif status := fwk.WaitOnPermit(ctx, assumedPod); !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n\t\t\t\tPod:         assumedPodInfo.Pod,\n\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap:      framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: status},\n\t\t\t\t\tUnschedulablePlugins: sets.New(status.Plugin()),\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn framework.NewStatus(status.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn status\n\t}\n\n\t// Run \"prebind\" plugins.\n\tif status := fwk.RunPreBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\treturn status\n\t}\n\n\t// Run \"bind\" plugins.\n\tif status := sched.bind(ctx, fwk, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, state); !status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\treturn status\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculating nodeResourceString can be heavy. Avoid it if klog verbosity is below 2.\n\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Successfully bound pod to node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(assumedPod), \"node\", scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, \"evaluatedNodes\", scheduleResult.EvaluatedNodes, \"feasibleNodes\", scheduleResult.FeasibleNodes)\n\tmetrics.PodScheduled(fwk.ProfileName(), metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n\tmetrics.PodSchedulingAttempts.Observe(float64(assumedPodInfo.Attempts))\n\tif assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp != nil {\n\t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n\t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingSLIDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n\t}\n\t// Run \"postbind\" plugins.\n\tfwk.RunPostBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\n\t// At the end of a successful binding cycle, move up Pods if needed.\n\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n\t\t// Unlike the logic in schedulingCycle(), we don't bother deleting the entries\n\t\t// as `podsToActivate.Map` is no longer consumed.\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) handleBindingCycleError(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n\tstart time.Time,\n\tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n\tstatus *framework.Status) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\n\tassumedPod := podInfo.Pod\n\t// trigger un-reserve plugins to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// \"Forget\"ing an assumed Pod in binding cycle should be treated as a PodDelete event,\n\t\t// as the assumed Pod had occupied a certain amount of resources in scheduler cache.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// Avoid moving the assumed Pod itself as it's always Unschedulable.\n\t\t// It's intentional to \"defer\" this operation; otherwise MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue() would\n\t\t// add this event to in-flight events and thus move the assumed pod to backoffQ anyways if the plugins don't have appropriate QueueingHint.\n\t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\tdefer sched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, internalqueue.AssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, func(pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\t\t\t\treturn assumedPod.UID != pod.UID\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, internalqueue.AssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, nil)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tsched.FailureHandler(ctx, fwk, podInfo, status, clearNominatedNode, start)\n}\n\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) frameworkForPod(pod *v1.Pod) (framework.Framework, error) {\n\tfwk, ok := sched.Profiles[pod.Spec.SchedulerName]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"profile not found for scheduler name %q\", pod.Spec.SchedulerName)\n\t}\n\treturn fwk, nil\n}\n\n// skipPodSchedule returns true if we could skip scheduling the pod for specified cases.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) skipPodSchedule(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\t// Case 1: pod is being deleted.\n\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n\t\tfwk.EventRecorder().Eventf(pod, nil, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"FailedScheduling\", \"Scheduling\", \"skip schedule deleting pod: %v/%v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name)\n\t\tklog.FromContext(ctx).V(3).Info(\"Skip schedule deleting pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\n\t// Case 2: pod that has been assumed could be skipped.\n\t// An assumed pod can be added again to the scheduling queue if it got an update event\n\t// during its previous scheduling cycle but before getting assumed.\n\tisAssumed, err := sched.Cache.IsAssumedPod(pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// TODO(91633): pass ctx into a revised HandleError\n\t\tutilruntime.HandleError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to check whether pod %s/%s is assumed: %v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name, err))\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn isAssumed\n}\n\n// schedulePod tries to schedule the given pod to one of the nodes in the node list.\n// If it succeeds, it will return the name of the node.\n// If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result ScheduleResult, err error) {\n\ttrace := utiltrace.New(\"Scheduling\", utiltrace.Field{Key: \"namespace\", Value: pod.Namespace}, utiltrace.Field{Key: \"name\", Value: pod.Name})\n\tdefer trace.LogIfLong(100 * time.Millisecond)\n\tif err := sched.Cache.UpdateSnapshot(klog.FromContext(ctx), sched.nodeInfoSnapshot); err != nil {\n\t\treturn result, err\n\t}\n\ttrace.Step(\"Snapshotting scheduler cache and node infos done\")\n\n\tif sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes() == 0 {\n\t\treturn result, ErrNoNodesAvailable\n\t}\n\n\tfeasibleNodes, diagnosis, err := sched.findNodesThatFitPod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn result, err\n\t}\n\ttrace.Step(\"Computing predicates done\")\n\n\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n\t\treturn result, &framework.FitError{\n\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n\t\t\tNumAllNodes: sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes(),\n\t\t\tDiagnosis:   diagnosis,\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// When only one node after predicate, just use it.\n\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 1 {\n\t\treturn ScheduleResult{\n\t\t\tSuggestedHost:  feasibleNodes[0].Node().Name,\n\t\t\tEvaluatedNodes: 1 + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n\t\t\tFeasibleNodes:  1,\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tpriorityList, err := prioritizeNodes(ctx, sched.Extenders, fwk, state, pod, feasibleNodes)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn result, err\n\t}\n\n\thost, _, err := selectHost(priorityList, numberOfHighestScoredNodesToReport)\n\ttrace.Step(\"Prioritizing done\")\n\n\treturn ScheduleResult{\n\t\tSuggestedHost:  host,\n\t\tEvaluatedNodes: len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n\t\tFeasibleNodes:  len(feasibleNodes),\n\t}, err\n}\n\n// Filters the nodes to find the ones that fit the pod based on the framework\n// filter plugins and filter extenders.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatFitPod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, framework.Diagnosis, error) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\tdiagnosis := framework.Diagnosis{\n\t\tNodeToStatusMap: make(framework.NodeToStatusMap),\n\t}\n\n\tallNodes, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NodeInfos().List()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n\t}\n\t// Run \"prefilter\" plugins.\n\tpreRes, s := fwk.RunPreFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod)\n\tif !s.IsSuccess() {\n\t\tif !s.IsRejected() {\n\t\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, s.AsError()\n\t\t}\n\t\t// All nodes in NodeToStatusMap will have the same status so that they can be handled in the preemption.\n\t\t// Some non trivial refactoring is needed to avoid this copy.\n\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = s\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Record the messages from PreFilter in Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg.\n\t\tmsg := s.Message()\n\t\tdiagnosis.PreFilterMsg = msg\n\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PreFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(s)\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// \"NominatedNodeName\" can potentially be set in a previous scheduling cycle as a result of preemption.\n\t// This node is likely the only candidate that will fit the pod, and hence we try it first before iterating over all nodes.\n\tif len(pod.Status.NominatedNodeName) > 0 {\n\t\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.evaluateNominatedNode(ctx, pod, fwk, state, diagnosis)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Evaluation failed on nominated node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", pod.Status.NominatedNodeName)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Nominated node passes all the filters, scheduler is good to assign this node to the pod.\n\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) != 0 {\n\t\t\treturn feasibleNodes, diagnosis, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnodes := allNodes\n\tif !preRes.AllNodes() {\n\t\tnodes = make([]*framework.NodeInfo, 0, len(preRes.NodeNames))\n\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n\t\t\tif !preRes.NodeNames.Has(n.Node().Name) {\n\t\t\t\t// We consider Nodes that are filtered out by PreFilterResult as rejected via UnschedulableAndUnresolvable.\n\t\t\t\t// We have to record them in NodeToStatusMap so that they won't be considered as candidates in the preemption.\n\t\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, \"node is filtered out by the prefilter result\")\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, nodes)\n\t// always try to update the sched.nextStartNodeIndex regardless of whether an error has occurred\n\t// this is helpful to make sure that all the nodes have a chance to be searched\n\tprocessedNodes := len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\tsched.nextStartNodeIndex = (sched.nextStartNodeIndex + processedNodes) % len(nodes)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n\t}\n\n\tfeasibleNodesAfterExtender, err := findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n\t}\n\tif len(feasibleNodesAfterExtender) != len(feasibleNodes) {\n\t\t// Extenders filtered out some nodes.\n\t\t//\n\t\t// Extender doesn't support any kind of requeueing feature like EnqueueExtensions in the scheduling framework.\n\t\t// When Extenders reject some Nodes and the pod ends up being unschedulable,\n\t\t// we put framework.ExtenderName to pInfo.UnschedulablePlugins.\n\t\t// This Pod will be requeued from unschedulable pod pool to activeQ/backoffQ\n\t\t// by any kind of cluster events.\n\t\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/122019\n\t\tif diagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins == nil {\n\t\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins = sets.New[string]()\n\t\t}\n\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins.Insert(framework.ExtenderName)\n\t}\n\n\treturn feasibleNodesAfterExtender, diagnosis, nil\n}\n\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) evaluateNominatedNode(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, diagnosis framework.Diagnosis) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n\tnnn := pod.Status.NominatedNodeName\n\tnodeInfo, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.Get(nnn)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tnode := []*framework.NodeInfo{nodeInfo}\n\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, node)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tfeasibleNodes, err = findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n}\n\n// hasScoring checks if scoring nodes is configured.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) hasScoring(fwk framework.Framework) bool {\n\tif fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n\t\tif extender.IsPrioritizer() {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// hasExtenderFilters checks if any extenders filter nodes.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) hasExtenderFilters() bool {\n\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n\t\tif extender.IsFilter() {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// findNodesThatPassFilters finds the nodes that fit the filter plugins.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatPassFilters(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tpod *v1.Pod,\n\tdiagnosis *framework.Diagnosis,\n\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n\tnumAllNodes := len(nodes)\n\tnumNodesToFind := sched.numFeasibleNodesToFind(fwk.PercentageOfNodesToScore(), int32(numAllNodes))\n\tif !sched.hasExtenderFilters() && !sched.hasScoring(fwk) {\n\t\tnumNodesToFind = 1\n\t}\n\n\t// Create feasible list with enough space to avoid growing it\n\t// and allow assigning.\n\tfeasibleNodes := make([]*framework.NodeInfo, numNodesToFind)\n\n\tif !fwk.HasFilterPlugins() {\n\t\tfor i := range feasibleNodes {\n\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[i] = nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n\t}\n\n\terrCh := parallelize.NewErrorChannel()\n\tvar feasibleNodesLen int32\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\ttype nodeStatus struct {\n\t\tnode   string\n\t\tstatus *framework.Status\n\t}\n\tresult := make([]*nodeStatus, numAllNodes)\n\tcheckNode := func(i int) {\n\t\t// We check the nodes starting from where we left off in the previous scheduling cycle,\n\t\t// this is to make sure all nodes have the same chance of being examined across pods.\n\t\tnodeInfo := nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n\t\tstatus := fwk.RunFilterPluginsWithNominatedPods(ctx, state, pod, nodeInfo)\n\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n\t\t\terrCh.SendErrorWithCancel(status.AsError(), cancel)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif status.IsSuccess() {\n\t\t\tlength := atomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, 1)\n\t\t\tif length > numNodesToFind {\n\t\t\t\tcancel()\n\t\t\t\tatomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, -1)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[length-1] = nodeInfo\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tresult[i] = &nodeStatus{node: nodeInfo.Node().Name, status: status}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tbeginCheckNode := time.Now()\n\tstatusCode := framework.Success\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\t// We record Filter extension point latency here instead of in framework.go because framework.RunFilterPlugins\n\t\t// function is called for each node, whereas we want to have an overall latency for all nodes per scheduling cycle.\n\t\t// Note that this latency also includes latency for `addNominatedPods`, which calls framework.RunPreFilterAddPod.\n\t\tmetrics.FrameworkExtensionPointDuration.WithLabelValues(metrics.Filter, statusCode.String(), fwk.ProfileName()).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(beginCheckNode))\n\t}()\n\n\t// Stops searching for more nodes once the configured number of feasible nodes\n\t// are found.\n\tfwk.Parallelizer().Until(ctx, numAllNodes, checkNode, metrics.Filter)\n\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleNodes[:feasibleNodesLen]\n\tfor _, item := range result {\n\t\tif item == nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[item.node] = item.status\n\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(item.status)\n\t}\n\tif err := errCh.ReceiveError(); err != nil {\n\t\tstatusCode = framework.Error\n\t\treturn feasibleNodes, err\n\t}\n\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n}\n\n// numFeasibleNodesToFind returns the number of feasible nodes that once found, the scheduler stops\n// its search for more feasible nodes.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) numFeasibleNodesToFind(percentageOfNodesToScore *int32, numAllNodes int32) (numNodes int32) {\n\tif numAllNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n\t\treturn numAllNodes\n\t}\n\n\t// Use profile percentageOfNodesToScore if it's set. Otherwise, use global percentageOfNodesToScore.\n\tvar percentage int32\n\tif percentageOfNodesToScore != nil {\n\t\tpercentage = *percentageOfNodesToScore\n\t} else {\n\t\tpercentage = sched.percentageOfNodesToScore\n\t}\n\n\tif percentage == 0 {\n\t\tpercentage = int32(50) - numAllNodes/125\n\t\tif percentage < minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind {\n\t\t\tpercentage = minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnumNodes = numAllNodes * percentage / 100\n\tif numNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n\t\treturn minFeasibleNodesToFind\n\t}\n\n\treturn numNodes\n}\n\nfunc findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx context.Context, extenders []framework.Extender, pod *v1.Pod, feasibleNodes []*framework.NodeInfo, statuses framework.NodeToStatusMap) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\t// Extenders are called sequentially.\n\t// Nodes in original feasibleNodes can be excluded in one extender, and pass on to the next\n\t// extender in a decreasing manner.\n\tfor _, extender := range extenders {\n\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !extender.IsInterested(pod) {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Status of failed nodes in failedAndUnresolvableMap will be added or overwritten in <statuses>,\n\t\t// so that the scheduler framework can respect the UnschedulableAndUnresolvable status for\n\t\t// particular nodes, and this may eventually improve preemption efficiency.\n\t\t// Note: users are recommended to configure the extenders that may return UnschedulableAndUnresolvable\n\t\t// status ahead of others.\n\t\tfeasibleList, failedMap, failedAndUnresolvableMap, err := extender.Filter(pod, feasibleNodes)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tif extender.IsIgnorable() {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping extender as it returned error and has ignorable flag set\", \"extender\", extender, \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor failedNodeName, failedMsg := range failedAndUnresolvableMap {\n\t\t\tvar aggregatedReasons []string\n\t\t\tif _, found := statuses[failedNodeName]; found {\n\t\t\t\taggregatedReasons = statuses[failedNodeName].Reasons()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\taggregatedReasons = append(aggregatedReasons, failedMsg)\n\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, aggregatedReasons...)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor failedNodeName, failedMsg := range failedMap {\n\t\t\tif _, found := failedAndUnresolvableMap[failedNodeName]; found {\n\t\t\t\t// failedAndUnresolvableMap takes precedence over failedMap\n\t\t\t\t// note that this only happens if the extender returns the node in both maps\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif _, found := statuses[failedNodeName]; !found {\n\t\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName] = framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable, failedMsg)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName].AppendReason(failedMsg)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleList\n\t}\n\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n}\n\n// prioritizeNodes prioritizes the nodes by running the score plugins,\n// which return a score for each node from the call to RunScorePlugins().\n// The scores from each plugin are added together to make the score for that node, then\n// any extenders are run as well.\n// All scores are finally combined (added) to get the total weighted scores of all nodes\nfunc prioritizeNodes(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\textenders []framework.Extender,\n\tfwk framework.Framework,\n\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n\tpod *v1.Pod,\n\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo,\n) ([]framework.NodePluginScores, error) {\n\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\t// If no priority configs are provided, then all nodes will have a score of one.\n\t// This is required to generate the priority list in the required format\n\tif len(extenders) == 0 && !fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n\t\tresult := make([]framework.NodePluginScores, 0, len(nodes))\n\t\tfor i := range nodes {\n\t\t\tresult = append(result, framework.NodePluginScores{\n\t\t\t\tName:       nodes[i].Node().Name,\n\t\t\t\tTotalScore: 1,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn result, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Run PreScore plugins.\n\tpreScoreStatus := fwk.RunPreScorePlugins(ctx, state, pod, nodes)\n\tif !preScoreStatus.IsSuccess() {\n\t\treturn nil, preScoreStatus.AsError()\n\t}\n\n\t// Run the Score plugins.\n\tnodesScores, scoreStatus := fwk.RunScorePlugins(ctx, state, pod, nodes)\n\tif !scoreStatus.IsSuccess() {\n\t\treturn nil, scoreStatus.AsError()\n\t}\n\n\t// Additional details logged at level 10 if enabled.\n\tloggerVTen := logger.V(10)\n\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n\t\tfor _, nodeScore := range nodesScores {\n\t\t\tfor _, pluginScore := range nodeScore.Scores {\n\t\t\t\tloggerVTen.Info(\"Plugin scored node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"plugin\", pluginScore.Name, \"node\", nodeScore.Name, \"score\", pluginScore.Score)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(extenders) != 0 && nodes != nil {\n\t\t// allNodeExtendersScores has all extenders scores for all nodes.\n\t\t// It is keyed with node name.\n\t\tallNodeExtendersScores := make(map[string]*framework.NodePluginScores, len(nodes))\n\t\tvar mu sync.Mutex\n\t\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n\t\tfor i := range extenders {\n\t\t\tif !extenders[i].IsInterested(pod) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\twg.Add(1)\n\t\t\tgo func(extIndex int) {\n\t\t\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.PrioritizingExtender).Inc()\n\t\t\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.PrioritizingExtender).Dec()\n\t\t\t\t\twg.Done()\n\t\t\t\t}()\n\t\t\t\tprioritizedList, weight, err := extenders[extIndex].Prioritize(pod, nodes)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Prioritization errors from extender can be ignored, let k8s/other extenders determine the priorities\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Failed to run extender's priority function. No score given by this extender.\", \"error\", err, \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"extender\", extenders[extIndex].Name())\n\t\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tmu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\tdefer mu.Unlock()\n\t\t\t\tfor i := range *prioritizedList {\n\t\t\t\t\tnodename := (*prioritizedList)[i].Host\n\t\t\t\t\tscore := (*prioritizedList)[i].Score\n\t\t\t\t\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tloggerVTen.Info(\"Extender scored node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"extender\", extenders[extIndex].Name(), \"node\", nodename, \"score\", score)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// MaxExtenderPriority may diverge from the max priority used in the scheduler and defined by MaxNodeScore,\n\t\t\t\t\t// therefore we need to scale the score returned by extenders to the score range used by the scheduler.\n\t\t\t\t\tfinalscore := score * weight * (framework.MaxNodeScore / extenderv1.MaxExtenderPriority)\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif allNodeExtendersScores[nodename] == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tallNodeExtendersScores[nodename] = &framework.NodePluginScores{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tName:   nodename,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tScores: make([]framework.PluginScore, 0, len(extenders)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tallNodeExtendersScores[nodename].Scores = append(allNodeExtendersScores[nodename].Scores, framework.PluginScore{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tName:  extenders[extIndex].Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\tScore: finalscore,\n\t\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t\t\tallNodeExtendersScores[nodename].TotalScore += finalscore\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}(i)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// wait for all go routines to finish\n\t\twg.Wait()\n\t\tfor i := range nodesScores {\n\t\t\tif score, ok := allNodeExtendersScores[nodes[i].Node().Name]; ok {\n\t\t\t\tnodesScores[i].Scores = append(nodesScores[i].Scores, score.Scores...)\n\t\t\t\tnodesScores[i].TotalScore += score.TotalScore\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n\t\tfor i := range nodesScores {\n\t\t\tloggerVTen.Info(\"Calculated node's final score for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", nodesScores[i].Name, \"score\", nodesScores[i].TotalScore)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nodesScores, nil\n}\n\nvar errEmptyPriorityList = errors.New(\"empty priorityList\")\n\n// selectHost takes a prioritized list of nodes and then picks one\n// in a reservoir sampling manner from the nodes that had the highest score.\n// It also returns the top {count} Nodes,\n// and the top of the list will be always the selected host.\nfunc selectHost(nodeScoreList []framework.NodePluginScores, count int) (string, []framework.NodePluginScores, error) {\n\tif len(nodeScoreList) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"\", nil, errEmptyPriorityList\n\t}\n\n\tvar h nodeScoreHeap = nodeScoreList\n\theap.Init(&h)\n\tcntOfMaxScore := 1\n\tselectedIndex := 0\n\t// The top of the heap is the NodeScoreResult with the highest score.\n\tsortedNodeScoreList := make([]framework.NodePluginScores, 0, count)\n\tsortedNodeScoreList = append(sortedNodeScoreList, heap.Pop(&h).(framework.NodePluginScores))\n\n\t// This for-loop will continue until all Nodes with the highest scores get checked for a reservoir sampling,\n\t// and sortedNodeScoreList gets (count - 1) elements.\n\tfor ns := heap.Pop(&h).(framework.NodePluginScores); ; ns = heap.Pop(&h).(framework.NodePluginScores) {\n\t\tif ns.TotalScore != sortedNodeScoreList[0].TotalScore && len(sortedNodeScoreList) == count {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif ns.TotalScore == sortedNodeScoreList[0].TotalScore {\n\t\t\tcntOfMaxScore++\n\t\t\tif rand.Intn(cntOfMaxScore) == 0 {\n\t\t\t\t// Replace the candidate with probability of 1/cntOfMaxScore\n\t\t\t\tselectedIndex = cntOfMaxScore - 1\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tsortedNodeScoreList = append(sortedNodeScoreList, ns)\n\n\t\tif h.Len() == 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif selectedIndex != 0 {\n\t\t// replace the first one with selected one\n\t\tprevious := sortedNodeScoreList[0]\n\t\tsortedNodeScoreList[0] = sortedNodeScoreList[selectedIndex]\n\t\tsortedNodeScoreList[selectedIndex] = previous\n\t}\n\n\tif len(sortedNodeScoreList) > count {\n\t\tsortedNodeScoreList = sortedNodeScoreList[:count]\n\t}\n\n\treturn sortedNodeScoreList[0].Name, sortedNodeScoreList, nil\n}\n\n// nodeScoreHeap is a heap of framework.NodePluginScores.\ntype nodeScoreHeap []framework.NodePluginScores\n\n// nodeScoreHeap implements heap.Interface.\nvar _ heap.Interface = &nodeScoreHeap{}\n\nfunc (h nodeScoreHeap) Len() int           { return len(h) }\nfunc (h nodeScoreHeap) Less(i, j int) bool { return h[i].TotalScore > h[j].TotalScore }\nfunc (h nodeScoreHeap) Swap(i, j int)      { h[i], h[j] = h[j], h[i] }\n\nfunc (h *nodeScoreHeap) Push(x interface{}) {\n\t*h = append(*h, x.(framework.NodePluginScores))\n}\n\nfunc (h *nodeScoreHeap) Pop() interface{} {\n\told := *h\n\tn := len(old)\n\tx := old[n-1]\n\t*h = old[0 : n-1]\n\treturn x\n}\n\n// assume signals to the cache that a pod is already in the cache, so that binding can be asynchronous.\n// assume modifies `assumed`.\nfunc (sched *Scheduler) assume(logger `ScheduleOne()` method (line 66)\n   - Pod with DRA device request cannot be scheduled because ResourceSlices don't exist yet\n   - Pod is marked as Unschedulable and added to unschedulable queue\n\n2. **Failure handling in**: `pkg/scheduler/schedule_one.go` - `handleSchedulingFailure()` method (line 1013)\n   - Calls `sched.SchedulingQueue.AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent()` to add pod to unschedulable queue\n\n3. **Pod re-evaluation triggered by**: `pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/scheduling_queue.go` - `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue()` (line 1120)\n   - This method should be called when ResourceSlice events occur\n   - It checks `isEventOfInterest()` to see if any plugin cares about the event\n\n4. **Event interest check in**: `pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/scheduling_queue.go` - `isEventOfInterest()` (line 414)\n   - Queries `p.queueingHintMap` to see if event is registered by any plugin\n   - If event is not in map, returns false and unschedulable pods stay unscheduled\n\n5. **Queueing hint map built from**: `pkg/scheduler/scheduler.go` - initialization (lines 315-320)\n   - Built from `buildQueueingHintMap(profile.EnqueueExtensions())`\n   - `EnqueueExtensions()` comes from plugins' `EventsToRegister()` methods\n\n6. **Event handlers registered by**: `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go` - `addAllEventHandlers()` (line 287)\n   - Iterates through `gvkMap` and registers event handlers\n   - Switch statement (line 396) handles known GVK types\n\n## Root Cause\n\n### **File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go`\n### **Function**: `EventsToRegister()` (line 381)\n### **Line**: ~410\n### **Explanation**:\nThe dynamicresources plugin does not register ResourceSlice events in its `EventsToRegister()` method. The method registers events for:\n- ResourceClaimParameters (line 389)\n- ResourceClassParameters (line 390)\n- ResourceClaim (line 393)\n- PodSchedulingContext (line 396)\n- Node (line 408)\n- ResourceClass (line 410)\n\n**But critically missing**: No registration for ResourceSlice events.\n\nWhen a DRA driver starts AFTER a pod has been created and marked as unschedulable, the driver creates ResourceSlice objects. However, because ResourceSlice is not in the queueing hint map, the `isEventOfInterest()` check at `pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/scheduling_queue.go:171` returns false, causing `movePodsToActiveOrBackoffQueue()` to return early without re-evaluating unschedulable pods.\n\n### **Secondary Issues**:\n\n1. **File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go`\n   - **Line**: ~96 (after ResourceClassParameters)\n   - **Issue**: No `ResourceSlice` GVK constant is defined\n   - All other DRA-related types are defined (ResourceClaim, ResourceClass, etc.) but ResourceSlice is missing\n\n2. **File**: `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go`\n   - **Function**: `addAllEventHandlers()`\n   - **Line**: ~515 (in the switch statement)\n   - **Issue**: No case for handling ResourceSlice events\n   - There's a case for each DRA type (PodSchedulingContext, ResourceClaim, ResourceClass, ResourceClaimParameters, ResourceClassParameters) but ResourceSlice is missing\n\n## Proposed Fix\n\nThe fix requires three changes:\n\n### 1. Add ResourceSlice GVK Constant\n**File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/types.go` (after line 96)\n\n```diff\n \tResourceClaim           GVK = \"ResourceClaim\"\n \tResourceClass           GVK = \"ResourceClass\"\n \tResourceClaimParameters GVK = \"ResourceClaimParameters\"\n \tResourceClassParameters GVK = \"ResourceClassParameters\"\n+\tResourceSlice           GVK = \"ResourceSlice\"\n```\n\n### 2. Register ResourceSlice Events in DRA Plugin\n**File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources/dynamicresources.go` (in EventsToRegister method, after line 410)\n\n```diff\n \tevents := []framework.ClusterEventWithHint{\n \t\t// Changes for claim or class parameters creation may make pods\n \t\t// schedulable which depend on claims using those parameters.\n \t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceClaimParameters, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}, QueueingHintFn: pl.isSchedulableAfterClaimParametersChange},\n \t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceClassParameters, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}, QueueingHintFn: pl.isSchedulableAfterClassParametersChange},\n\n \t\t// Allocation is tracked in ResourceClaims, so any changes may make the pods schedulable.\n \t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceClaim, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}, QueueingHintFn: pl.isSchedulableAfterClaimChange},\n \t\t// When a driver has provided additional information, a pod waiting for that information\n \t\t// may be schedulable.\n \t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.PodSchedulingContext, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}, QueueingHintFn: pl.isSchedulableAfterPodSchedulingContextChange},\n+\t\t// ResourceSlices provide the actual resource availability on nodes.\n+\t\t// When a new ResourceSlice is available or updated, pods waiting for those resources\n+\t\t// may become schedulable.\n+\t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceSlice, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}, QueueingHintFn: pl.isSchedulableAfterResourceSliceChange},\n \t\t// A resource might depend on node labels for topology filtering.\n \t\t// A new or updated node may make pods schedulable.\n \t\t//\n \t\t// A note about UpdateNodeTaint event:\n \t\t// NodeAdd QueueingHint isn't always called because of the internal feature called preCheck.\n \t\t// As a common problematic scenario,\n \t\t// when a node is added but not ready, NodeAdd event is filtered out by preCheck and doesn't arrive.\n \t\t// In such cases, this plugin may miss some events that actually make pods schedulable.\n \t\t// As a workaround, we add UpdateNodeTaint event to catch the case.\n \t\t// We can remove UpdateNodeTaint when we remove the preCheck feature.\n \t\t// See: https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/110175\n \t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.Node, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.UpdateNodeLabel | framework.UpdateNodeTaint}},\n \t\t// A pod might be waiting for a class to get created or modified.\n \t\t{Event: framework.ClusterEvent{Resource: framework.ResourceClass, ActionType: framework.Add | framework.Update}},\n \t}\n```\n\nAlso add the queueing hint function:\n\n```diff\n // isSchedulableAfterPodSchedulingContextChange is invoked for add and update PodSchedulingContext events.\n // It checks whether that change made a previously unschedulable pod schedulable.\n func (pl *dynamicResources) isSchedulableAfterPodSchedulingContextChange(logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, oldObj, newObj interface{}) (framework.QueueingHint, error) {\n \t// ... existing implementation\n }\n\n+// isSchedulableAfterResourceSliceChange is invoked for add and update ResourceSlice events.\n+// It checks whether that change made a previously unschedulable pod schedulable.\n+// ResourceSlice changes are relevant for all pods using dynamic resources, as they may affect\n+// which resources are available for allocation.\n+func (pl *dynamicResources) isSchedulableAfterResourceSliceChange(logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, oldObj, newObj interface{}) (framework.QueueingHint, error) {\n+\t// If the pod doesn't use resource claims, it's not affected by ResourceSlice changes\n+\tif err := pl.foreachPodResourceClaim(pod, nil); err != nil {\n+\t\t// Pod has no resource claims, ResourceSlice change is not relevant\n+\t\treturn framework.QueueSkip, nil\n+\t}\n+\t// ResourceSlice changes may affect available resources, so we queue the pod\n+\t// to re-evaluate scheduling. This is especially important when a DRA driver\n+\t// starts after the pod and publishes ResourceSlice objects.\n+\treturn framework.Queue, nil\n+}\n```\n\n### 3. Add Event Handler for ResourceSlice\n**File**: `pkg/scheduler/eventhandlers.go` (in addAllEventHandlers switch statement, after ResourceClassParameters case at line 492)\n\n```diff\n \t\tcase framework.ResourceClassParameters:\n \t\t\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {\n \t\t\t\tif handlerRegistration, err = informerFactory.Resource().V1alpha2().ResourceClassParameters().Informer().AddEventHandler(\n \t\t\t\t\tbuildEvtResHandler(at, framework.ResourceClassParameters, \"ResourceClassParameters\"),\n \t\t\t\t); err != nil {\n+\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n+\t\t\t\t}\n+\t\t\t\thandlers = append(handlers, handlerRegistration)\n+\t\t\t}\n \t\tcase framework.StorageClass:\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### The Race Condition\n\nThe bug is a classic race condition in event-driven architectures:\n\n1. **Working case (driver starts first)**:\n   - Driver starts and creates ResourceSlice objects\n   - Pod is created, requests DRA resources\n   - Scheduler sees ResourceSlices exist and schedules pod successfully\n\n2. **Broken case (pod created first)**:\n   - Pod is created requesting DRA resources\n   - Scheduler attempts scheduling, no ResourceSlices exist yet\n   - Scheduling fails with \"cannot allocate all claims\" → pod marked Unschedulable\n   - Pod added to unschedulable queue\n   - Driver starts and creates ResourceSlice objects\n   - ResourceSlice events are emitted BUT...\n   - No event handler registered for ResourceSlice in the scheduler\n   - `isEventOfInterest()` check returns false for ResourceSlice events\n   - `movePodsToActiveOrBackoffQueue()` returns early at line 1171\n   - Unschedulable pods are never re-evaluated\n   - **Pod stuck in Pending/Unschedulable state forever**\n\n### Why This Happened\n\nThe DynamicResourceAllocation feature was developed with multiple types of events:\n- ResourceClaim: tracks allocation status\n- ResourceClaimParameters: parameter changes\n- ResourceClassParameters: parameter changes\n- ResourceClass: class creation/modification\n- PodSchedulingContext: driver status/resource hints\n\nHowever, ResourceSlice (which actually advertises available resources on nodes) was not included in the event registration. This is a critical oversight because:\n\n1. ResourceSlice is the actual signal that resources are available\n2. Without it, the scheduler has no way to know that a DRA driver has started and made resources available\n3. The unschedulable pod re-evaluation mechanism silently ignores ResourceSlice events because they're not in the queueing hint map\n\n### The Fix\n\nThe fix adds ResourceSlice to the event handling pipeline at three levels:\n\n1. **GVK definition**: Makes ResourceSlice a known resource type in the scheduler framework\n2. **Plugin event registration**: The DRA plugin declares that it cares about ResourceSlice events (Add and Update actions)\n3. **Event handler registration**: The scheduler registers informer event handlers to forward ResourceSlice events to the scheduling queue\n4. **Queueing hint function**: Provides logic to determine if a ResourceSlice event should trigger pod re-scheduling\n\nThis ensures that when a DRA driver publishes ResourceSlices, the scheduler's scheduling queue is notified via `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue()`, checks `isEventOfInterest()` (which now returns true), and moves waiting unschedulable pods back to the active queue for re-evaluation.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":538,"cache_read_input_tokens":56691,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":538},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"bf859bd5-e665-429c-be32-3628bed434ac","uuid":"cda25169-2564-47a9-b8a8-cf74cae703d8"}

err != nil {\n \t\t\t\t\treturn err\n \t\t\t\t}\n \t\t\t\thandlers = append(handlers, handlerRegistration)\n \t\t\t}\n+\t\tcase framework.ResourceSlice:\n+\t\t\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.DynamicResourceAllocation) {\n+\t\t\t\tif handlerRegistration, err = informerFactory.Resource().V1alpha2().ResourceSlices().Informer().AddEventHandler(\n+\t\t\t\t\tbuildEvtResHandler(at, framework.ResourceSlice, \"ResourceSlice\"),\n+\t\t\t\t); err != nil {\n+\t\t\t\t\treturn err\n+\t\t\t\t}\n+\t\t\t\thandlers = append(handlers, handlerRegistration)\n+\t\t\t}\n \t\tcase framework.StorageClass:\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### The Race Condition\n\nThe bug is a classic race condition in event-driven architectures:\n\n1. **Working case (driver starts first)**:\n   - Driver starts and creates ResourceSlice objects\n   - Pod is created, requests DRA resources\n   - Scheduler sees ResourceSlices exist and schedules pod successfully\n\n2. **Broken case (pod created first)**:\n   - Pod is created requesting DRA resources\n   - Scheduler attempts scheduling, no ResourceSlices exist yet\n   - Scheduling fails with \"cannot allocate all claims\" → pod marked Unschedulable\n   - Pod added to unschedulable queue\n   - Driver starts and creates ResourceSlice objects\n   - ResourceSlice events are emitted BUT...\n   - No event handler registered for ResourceSlice in the scheduler\n   - `isEventOfInterest()` check returns false for ResourceSlice events\n   - `movePodsToActiveOrBackoffQueue()` returns early at line 1171\n   - Unschedulable pods are never re-evaluated\n   - **Pod stuck in Pending/Unschedulable state forever**\n\n### Why This Happened\n\nThe DynamicResourceAllocation feature was developed with multiple types of events:\n- ResourceClaim: tracks allocation status\n- ResourceClaimParameters: parameter changes\n- ResourceClassParameters: parameter changes\n- ResourceClass: class creation/modification\n- PodSchedulingContext: driver status/resource hints\n\nHowever, ResourceSlice (which actually advertises available resources on nodes) was not included in the event registration. This is a critical oversight because:\n\n1. ResourceSlice is the actual signal that resources are available\n2. Without it, the scheduler has no way to know that a DRA driver has started and made resources available\n3. The unschedulable pod re-evaluation mechanism silently ignores ResourceSlice events because they're not in the queueing hint map\n\n### The Fix\n\nThe fix adds ResourceSlice to the event handling pipeline at three levels:\n\n1. **GVK definition**: Makes ResourceSlice a known resource type in the scheduler framework\n2. **Plugin event registration**: The DRA plugin declares that it cares about ResourceSlice events (Add and Update actions)\n3. **Event handler registration**: The scheduler registers informer event handlers to forward ResourceSlice events to the scheduling queue\n4. **Queueing hint function**: Provides logic to determine if a ResourceSlice event should trigger pod re-scheduling\n\nThis ensures that when a DRA driver publishes ResourceSlices, the scheduler's scheduling queue is notified via `MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue()`, checks `isEventOfInterest()` (which now returns true), and moves waiting unschedulable pods back to the active queue for re-evaluation.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
